,,,,,,,<h1>The Prince Is Dead</h1> <h2>-60 km: A Shared Sanctum</h2> (if:$trigFlag is 1)[(set:$trigFlag to 0)(save-game:"starterSave")] No matter how hard you try, you can never truly escape your position in The Abyss. While your father and his army of bureaucrats spend their solstice toiling away in the extravagant, scorching halls of the core, you have retreated towards the surface, finding some respite in the dark, barren tunnels of the Abyssal Dungeon. Father has never //approved// of your escapades, but the imps who guard the dungeon have grown a fondness for your company. While you have no need for their protection, companionship is hard to come by for you, so you don't mind. One of your biggest hassles as the Demon King's daughter comes from your father's delegated paperwork. Since your father has co-opted your escapism into his logistical schemes, messengers usually bother ''you'' when they don't want to wait in line at the core. Today, it's a stout, eagle-headed fiend. He most likely represents the aggressive party in some petty squabble between a couple of merchants. You don't particularly care. You've never been given much of a choice in this. You take the quill from his hand and on the line you sloppily sign... One day, as you were harvesting herbs together, he admitted the truth: Your father kept the garden as a sanctum of sorts, the lone place he could escape his guards. You missed that side of him as you grew older and saw it less... When your time came, you took the name Basilia, declaring yourself the one herb which The Abyss grew in secret to even //him//. You go bright red to signal defeat... but you don't pull your hand back. Your moment is interrupted by a small tut from a staff member. "Oh dear, if it isn't Ms. $Name. To what do we owe the honor?" A tall fiend approaches and gives a mocking bow. "Oh, uh.. hey Xana... this is Ariadne... we're just here for a meal..." It's hard to talk much with Xanaphos staring you down. They've got just a few too many eyes, all attached to a brain that's come to know you a //bit// too well over the years. "Oh well isn't that just precious? I'm glad you're getting out of that study more often, doll. I don't care what your pops thinks, that's no place for a growing woman to spend her days." Xana gives you a sly grin. You don't particularly like that they're right. Luckily, they leave you be after taking down some drinks for the both of you. Xana is silent when they return with Ari's coffee and your tea, and Ari breaks the silence once they're out of earshot.. "Uhm... what did they mean about your study? If... if it's not prying..." Ari twirls her hair in her finger. She always seems very scared to ask you too many personal questions. You probably shouldn't tell her all that you do, but... you just can't help it with her.
